[2025-12-14 09:49:45.127113] Forwarded to 2756430740: 🔻🇮🇳📵 **BIG CHANGE |DoT** Mandates Active SIM for Messaging Apps

The Department of Telecommunications (DoT) has issued new directives mandating that **messaging/communication apps** — including **WhatsApp, Telegram, Signal, Snapchat, ShareChat, JioChat, Arattai, Josh** and others can **only be used with an active SIM card in the device**.

**Key Points:**
• Apps must not run without a **live SIM** in the device
• All platforms must file **compliance reports within 120 days**
• Non-compliance will attract action under the **Telecom Act 2023** & **Cyber Security Rules**
• Web logins will **auto-expire every 6 hours**, requiring QR re-authentication
• Apps now classified as **Telecom Identifier User Entities (TIUEs)**
• Rules aim to stop **cross-border misuse**, cyber-frauds & untraceable logins
• New measures include **Mobile Number Validation**, **Resale Device Scrubbing**, and stricter **IMEI tracking**

The directive is part of the **TCS Amendment Rules 2025**, aimed at strengthening cyber security and preventing telecom-identifier fraud.
